\end{DoxyCompactItemize}


\subsection{\-Detailed \-Description}
\-Partial implementation of \-M\-P\-I using only threads. \-See the \-M\-P\-I specification at \href{http://www.mpi-forum.org/docs/docs.html}{\tt http\-://www.\-mpi-\/forum.\-org/docs/docs.\-html} for an explanation of what these functions do.

\-Because this is a thread-\/based library, be very careful with global variables and static variables in functions\-: they will be shared across all threads and lead to conflicts if not properly mutex-\/ed or barrier-\/ed out.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{\-See also}
\href{http://www.mpi-forum.org/docs/docs.html}{\tt http\-://www.\-mpi-\/forum.\-org/docs/docs.\-html} for \-M\-P\-I documentation. 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\index{t\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-Status@{t\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-Status}!include/thread_mpi/tmpi.h@{include/thread\-\_\-mpi/tmpi.\-h}}
\subsubsection[{t\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-Status}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}typedef struct {\bf tmpi\-\_\-status\-\_\-}  {\bf t\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-Status}}}\label{include_2thread__mpi_2tmpi_8h_a531b9d68a797b1d19168df2fd83cb8aa}
t\-M\-P\-I \-Status.

\-Holds status info (tag, sender, amount of data transmitted) for receives. \-The status object is user-\/maintained.

\hypertarget{include_2thread__mpi_2tmpi_8h_addb14c251e4805bc95120dc0cb90849f}{\index{include/thread\-\_\-mpi/tmpi.\-h@{include/thread\-\_\-mpi/tmpi.\-h}!t\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-Affinity\-\_\-strategy@{t\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-Affinity\-\_\-strategy}}
\index{t\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-Affinity\-\_\-strategy@{t\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-Affinity\-\_\-strategy}!include/thread_mpi/tmpi.h@{include/thread\-\_\-mpi/tmpi.\-h}}
\subsubsection[{t\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-Affinity\-\_\-strategy}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}enum {\bf t\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-Affinity\-\_\-strategy}}}\label{include_2thread__mpi_2tmpi_8h_addb14c251e4805bc95120dc0cb90849f}
t\-M\-P\-I initialization thread affinity strategy.

\-Used in the t\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-Init\-\_\-affinity() and t\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-Init\-\_\-fn\-\_\-affinity() functions, to control how affinity is set. \-The default \hyperlink{include_2thread__mpi_2tmpi_8h_ae84ee78d835a33e3f1918e2dd455de1e}{t\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-Init()} and \hyperlink{include_2thread__mpi_2tmpi_8h_ab3fea8b342f7c7de0dbb07c30afcfa7a}{t\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-Init\-\_\-fn()} functions use the \-T\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-A\-F\-F\-I\-N\-I\-T\-Y\-\_\-\-A\-L\-L\-\_\-\-C\-O\-R\-E\-S strategy.

\-These strategies are fairly basic. \-For more flexibility, use the t\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-Set\-\_\-affinity() function. \begin{Desc}
\item[\-Enumerator\-: ]\par
\begin{description}
\index{\-T\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-A\-F\-F\-I\-N\-I\-T\-Y\-\_\-\-N\-O\-N\-E@{\-T\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-A\-F\-F\-I\-N\-I\-T\-Y\-\_\-\-N\-O\-N\-E}!include/thread\-\_\-mpi/tmpi.\-h@{include/thread\-\_\-mpi/tmpi.\-h}}\index{include/thread\-\_\-mpi/tmpi.\-h@{include/thread\-\_\-mpi/tmpi.\-h}!\-T\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-A\-F\-F\-I\-N\-I\-T\-Y\-\_\-\-N\-O\-N\-E@{\-T\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-A\-F\-F\-I\-N\-I\-T\-Y\-\_\-\-N\-O\-N\-E}}\item[{\em 
\hypertarget{include_2thread__mpi_2tmpi_8h_addb14c251e4805bc95120dc0cb90849facb60f20cc2c56e7f274738333af272a3}{\-T\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-A\-F\-F\-I\-N\-I\-T\-Y\-\_\-\-N\-O\-N\-E}\label{include_2thread__mpi_2tmpi_8h_addb14c251e4805bc95120dc0cb90849facb60f20cc2c56e7f274738333af272a3}
}]\-Do not set any thread affinity \index{\-T\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-A\-F\-F\-I\-N\-I\-T\-Y\-\_\-\-A\-L\-L\-\_\-\-C\-O\-R\-E\-S@{\-T\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-A\-F\-F\-I\-N\-I\-T\-Y\-\_\-\-A\-L\-L\-\_\-\-C\-O\-R\-E\-S}!include/thread\-\_\-mpi/tmpi.\-h@{include/thread\-\_\-mpi/tmpi.\-h}}\index{include/thread\-\_\-mpi/tmpi.\-h@{include/thread\-\_\-mpi/tmpi.\-h}!\-T\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-A\-F\-F\-I\-N\-I\-T\-Y\-\_\-\-A\-L\-L\-\_\-\-C\-O\-R\-E\-S@{\-T\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-A\-F\-F\-I\-N\-I\-T\-Y\-\_\-\-A\-L\-L\-\_\-\-C\-O\-R\-E\-S}}\item[{\em 
\hypertarget{include_2thread__mpi_2tmpi_8h_addb14c251e4805bc95120dc0cb90849fa23e19470a00d63500440b52a1b08994d}{\-T\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-A\-F\-F\-I\-N\-I\-T\-Y\-\_\-\-A\-L\-L\-\_\-\-C\-O\-R\-E\-S}\label{include_2thread__mpi_2tmpi_8h_addb14c251e4805bc95120dc0cb90849fa23e19470a00d63500440b52a1b08994d}
}]\-Only set affinity if the number of threads is equal to the number of hardware threads (cores + hyperthreads). \-This is the only safe way to set thread affinity, without clashes between multiple instances of the same program. \index{\-T\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-A\-F\-F\-I\-N\-I\-T\-Y\-\_\-\-N\-O\-N\-E@{\-T\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-A\-F\-F\-I\-N\-I\-T\-Y\-\_\-\-N\-O\-N\-E}!include/thread\-\_\-mpi/tmpi.\-h@{include/thread\-\_\-mpi/tmpi.\-h}}\index{include/thread\-\_\-mpi/tmpi.\-h@{include/thread\-\_\-mpi/tmpi.\-h}!\-T\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-A\-F\-F\-I\-N\-I\-T\-Y\-\_\-\-N\-O\-N\-E@{\-T\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-A\-F\-F\-I\-N\-I\-T\-Y\-\_\-\-N\-O\-N\-E}}\item[{\em 
\hypertarget{include_2thread__mpi_2tmpi_8h_addb14c251e4805bc95120dc0cb90849facb60f20cc2c56e7f274738333af272a3}{\-T\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-A\-F\-F\-I\-N\-I\-T\-Y\-\_\-\-N\-O\-N\-E}\label{include_2thread__mpi_2tmpi_8h_addb14c251e4805bc95120dc0cb90849facb60f20cc2c56e7f274738333af272a3}
}]\-Do not set any thread affinity \index{\-T\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-A\-F\-F\-I\-N\-I\-T\-Y\-\_\-\-A\-L\-L\-\_\-\-C\-O\-R\-E\-S@{\-T\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-A\-F\-F\-I\-N\-I\-T\-Y\-\_\-\-A\-L\-L\-\_\-\-C\-O\-R\-E\-S}!include/thread\-\_\-mpi/tmpi.\-h@{include/thread\-\_\-mpi/tmpi.\-h}}\index{include/thread\-\_\-mpi/tmpi.\-h@{include/thread\-\_\-mpi/tmpi.\-h}!\-T\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-A\-F\-F\-I\-N\-I\-T\-Y\-\_\-\-A\-L\-L\-\_\-\-C\-O\-R\-E\-S@{\-T\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-A\-F\-F\-I\-N\-I\-T\-Y\-\_\-\-A\-L\-L\-\_\-\-C\-O\-R\-E\-S}}\item[{\em 
\hypertarget{include_2thread__mpi_2tmpi_8h_addb14c251e4805bc95120dc0cb90849fa23e19470a00d63500440b52a1b08994d}{\-T\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-A\-F\-F\-I\-N\-I\-T\-Y\-\_\-\-A\-L\-L\-\_\-\-C\-O\-R\-E\-S}\label{include_2thread__mpi_2tmpi_8h_addb14c251e4805bc95120dc0cb90849fa23e19470a00d63500440b52a1b08994d}
}]\-Only set affinity if the number of threads is equal to the number of hardware threads (cores + hyperthreads). \-This is the only safe way to set thread affinity, without clashes between multiple instances of the same program. \end{description}
\end{Desc}

\-Just kills all threads.

\-Not really neccesary because exit() would do that for us anyway.

\-Do an operation between all locally held buffers on all items in the buffers and broadcast the results.

\-Collective function.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{\-Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em sendbuf} & \-The operand parameters. \-Any process may specify \-T\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-I\-N\-\_\-\-P\-L\-A\-C\-E, in which case recvbuf will hold the operand parameters for that process. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in,out}  & {\em recvbuf} & \-The result buffer. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em count} & \-The number of items to do operation on. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em datatype} & \-The data type of the items. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em op} & \-The operation to perform. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em comm} & \-The communicator.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\-T\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-S\-U\-C\-C\-E\-S\-S on success, \-T\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-F\-A\-I\-L\-U\-R\-E on failure. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

)}}\label{include_2thread__mpi_2tmpi_8h_a4f139d59e3788d0ce8074d786c312966}
\-Broadcast from one thread to all others in comm.

\-Collective function; data is transferred from root's buffer to all others' buffer.

\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\hypertarget{include_2thread__mpi_2tmpi_8h_a4e3b45f7896f31ab65ff9cbb8a72a9ff}{\index{include/thread\-\_\-mpi/tmpi.\-h@{include/thread\-\_\-mpi/tmpi.\-h}!t\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-Comm\-\_\-split@{t\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-Comm\-\_\-split}}
\index{t\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-Comm\-\_\-split@{t\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-Comm\-\_\-split}!include/thread_mpi/tmpi.h@{include/thread\-\_\-mpi/tmpi.\-h}}
\subsubsection[{t\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-Comm\-\_\-split}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}{\bf \-T\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-E\-X\-P\-O\-R\-T} int {\bf t\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-Comm\-\_\-split} (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf t\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-Comm}}]{comm, }
\item[{int}]{color, }
\item[{int}]{key, }
\item[{{\bf t\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-Comm} $\ast$}]{newcomm}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{include_2thread__mpi_2tmpi_8h_a4e3b45f7896f31ab65ff9cbb8a72a9ff}
\-Split up a group into same-\/colored sub-\/groups ordered by key.

\-This is the main comm creation function\-: it's a collective call that takes a color and a key from each process, and arranges all threads that call t\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-Split() withe the same color together into a comm.

\-The rank in the new group will be based on the value given in key.

\-Passing \-T\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-U\-N\-D\-E\-F\-I\-N\-E\-D as a color will result in the thread not being part of any group, and getting \-T\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-C\-O\-M\-M\-\_\-\-N\-U\-L\-L back in newcomm.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{\-Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em comm} & \-The originating comm. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em color} & \-This thread's color (determines which comm it will be in). \-Giving \-T\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-U\-N\-D\-E\-F\-I\-N\-E\-D will result in this thread not being in any group. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em key} & \-This thread's key (determines rank). \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt out}  & {\em newcomm} & \-The new comm. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{\-Returns}
\-T\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-S\-U\-C\-C\-E\-S\-S on success, \-T\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-F\-A\-I\-L\-U\-R\-E on failure. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\end{figure}

)}}\label{include_2thread__mpi_2tmpi_8h_af00dc1f596635c23a3779986e5ef2cdc}
\-Gather data from all threads in comm to root.

\-Collective function; assumes that all data is received in blocks of recvcount.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{\-Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em sendbuf} & \-The send buffer for all threads (root may specify \-T\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-I\-N\-\_\-\-P\-L\-A\-C\-E, in which case it transfers nothing to itself). \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em sendcount} & \-The number of items to send for all threads. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em sendtype} & \-The type of the items to send. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt out}  & {\em recvbuf} & \-The receiving buffer (for root thread). \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em recvcount} & \-The number of items to receive (for root). \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em recvtype} & \-The type of the items to receive (for root). \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em root} & \-The rank of root. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em comm} & \-The communicator.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{\-Returns}
\-T\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-S\-U\-C\-C\-E\-S\-S on success, \-T\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-F\-A\-I\-L\-U\-R\-E on failure. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{include_2thread__mpi_2tmpi_8h_a8e0f9010201a90f96c23f2c3684b526b}
\-Gather irregularly laid out data from all processes in comm to root.

\-Collective function.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{\-Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em sendbuf} & \-The send buffer for all threads (root may specify \-T\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-I\-N\-\_\-\-P\-L\-A\-C\-E, in which case it transfers nothing to itself). \\
\hline

\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em sendtype} & \-The type of the items to send. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt out}  & {\em recvbuf} & \-The receiving buffer (for root thread). \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em recvcounts} & \-The list of number of items to receive (for root). \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em displs} & \-The list of displacements in recvbuf to receive data in (for root). \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em recvtype} & \-The type of the items to receive (for root). \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em root} & \-The rank of root. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em comm} & \-The communicator.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\hypertarget{include_2thread__mpi_2tmpi_8h_ae84ee78d835a33e3f1918e2dd455de1e}{\index{include/thread\-\_\-mpi/tmpi.\-h@{include/thread\-\_\-mpi/tmpi.\-h}!t\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-Init@{t\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-Init}}
\index{t\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-Init@{t\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-Init}!include/thread_mpi/tmpi.h@{include/thread\-\_\-mpi/tmpi.\-h}}
\subsubsection[{t\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-Init}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}{\bf \-T\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-E\-X\-P\-O\-R\-T} int {\bf t\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-Init} (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{int $\ast$}]{argc, }
\item[{char $\ast$$\ast$$\ast$}]{argv, }
\item[{int($\ast$)(int, char $\ast$$\ast$)}]{start\-\_\-function}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{include_2thread__mpi_2tmpi_8h_ae84ee78d835a33e3f1918e2dd455de1e}
\-Traditional \-M\-P\-I initializer; spawns threads that start at the given function.

\-Seeks the argument '-\/nt n', where n is the number of threads that will be created. \-If n==0, the number of threads will be the recommended number of threads for this platform as obtained from t\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-Get\-\_\-recommended\-\_\-ntreads().

\-The new threads then run the function start\-\_\-function, with the original argc and argv. \-This function could be \hyperlink{TestAtomics_8c_a840291bc02cba5474a4cb46a9b9566fe}{main()}, or any other function; calling this function again -\/ whether from the started threads or from the main thread -\/ has no effect.

\-On platforms that support thread affinity setting, this function will use the 'all-\/cores' affinity strategy\-: it will only set thread affinity if the number of threads is equal to the number of hardware threads (cores + hyperthreads).


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{\-Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em argc} & argc of original \hyperlink{TestAtomics_8c_a840291bc02cba5474a4cb46a9b9566fe}{main()} invocation, or \-N\-U\-L\-L \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em argv} & argv of original \hyperlink{TestAtomics_8c_a840291bc02cba5474a4cb46a9b9566fe}{main()} invocation, or \-N\-U\-L\-L. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em start\-\_\-function} & \-Starting function of type int start\-\_\-function(int argc, char $\ast$argv\mbox{[}$\,$\mbox{]});\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{\-Returns}
\-T\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-S\-U\-C\-C\-E\-S\-S on success, \-T\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-F\-A\-I\-L\-U\-R\-E on failure. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\hypertarget{include_2thread__mpi_2tmpi_8h_ab3fea8b342f7c7de0dbb07c30afcfa7a}{\index{include/thread\-\_\-mpi/tmpi.\-h@{include/thread\-\_\-mpi/tmpi.\-h}!t\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-Init\-\_\-fn@{t\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-Init\-\_\-fn}}
\index{t\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-Init\-\_\-fn@{t\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-Init\-\_\-fn}!include/thread_mpi/tmpi.h@{include/thread\-\_\-mpi/tmpi.\-h}}
\subsubsection[{t\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-Init\-\_\-fn}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}{\bf \-T\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-E\-X\-P\-O\-R\-T} int {\bf t\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-Init\-\_\-fn} (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{int}]{main\-\_\-thread\-\_\-returns, }
\item[{int}]{\-N, }
\item[{{\bf t\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-Affinity\-\_\-strategy}}]{aff\-\_\-strategy, }
\item[{{\bf void}($\ast$)({\bf void} $\ast$)}]{start\-\_\-function, }
\item[{{\bf void} $\ast$}]{arg}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{include_2thread__mpi_2tmpi_8h_ab3fea8b342f7c7de0dbb07c30afcfa7a}
\-Generic init function thread \-M\-P\-I intializer and thread spawner.

\-Creates \-N threads (including main thread) that run the function start\-\_\-function, which takes a void$\ast$ argument, given by arg. \-The function start\-\_\-function also gets called by the main thread. \-When the function start\-\_\-function returns it, will behave as if t\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-Finalize is called, and if it's a sub-\/thread it will stop running.

\-If \-N==0, the number of threads will be the recommended number of threads for this platform as obtained from t\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-Get\-\_\-recommended\-\_\-ntreads().

\-Note that thread affinity strategy only has an effect when this is supported by the underlying platform. \-As of yet (2012), this is not the case for \-Mac \-O\-S \-X, for example.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{\-Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em main\-\_\-thread\-\_\-returns} & whether the control in the main thread should return immediately (if true), or the start\-\_\-function() should be called from the main thread, too (if false). \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em \-N} & \-The number of threads to start (or 0 to automatically determine this). \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em aff\-\_\-strategy} & \-The thread affinity strategy to use. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em start\-\_\-function} & \-The function to start threads at (including main thread if main\-\_\-thread\-\_\-returns). \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em arg} & \-An optional argument for start\-\_\-function().\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{\-Returns}
\-T\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-F\-A\-I\-L\-U\-R\-E on failure, \-T\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-S\-U\-C\-C\-E\-S\-S on succes (after all threads have finished if main\-\_\-thread\-\_\-returns=true). 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\hypertarget{include_2thread__mpi_2tmpi_8h_ae913220747395bc0022cf2f3ceac9046}{\index{include/thread\-\_\-mpi/tmpi.\-h@{include/thread\-\_\-mpi/tmpi.\-h}!t\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-Initialized@{t\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-Initialized}}
\index{t\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-Initialized@{t\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-Initialized}!include/thread_mpi/tmpi.h@{include/thread\-\_\-mpi/tmpi.\-h}}
\subsubsection[{t\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-Initialized}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}{\bf \-T\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-E\-X\-P\-O\-R\-T} int {\bf t\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-Initialized} (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{int $\ast$}]{flag}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{include_2thread__mpi_2tmpi_8h_ae913220747395bc0022cf2f3ceac9046}
whether t\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-Init, but not yet t\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-Finalize, has been run


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{\-Parameters}
\mbox{\tt out}  & {\em flag} & \-Set to \-T\-R\-U\-E if \hyperlink{include_2thread__mpi_2tmpi_8h_ae84ee78d835a33e3f1918e2dd455de1e}{t\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-Init()} has been called, \-F\-A\-L\-S\-E if not.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

always returns \-T\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-S\-U\-C\-C\-E\-S\-S. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\hypertarget{include_2thread__mpi_2tmpi_8h_a839030e4e95e6d349f4888697b5aee2c}{\index{include/thread\-\_\-mpi/tmpi.\-h@{include/thread\-\_\-mpi/tmpi.\-h}!t\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-Irecv@{t\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-Irecv}}
\index{t\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-Irecv@{t\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-Irecv}!include/thread_mpi/tmpi.h@{include/thread\-\_\-mpi/tmpi.\-h}}
\subsubsection[{t\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-Irecv}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}{\bf \-T\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-E\-X\-P\-O\-R\-T} int {\bf t\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-Irecv} (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf void} $\ast$}]{buf, }
\item[{int}]{count, }
\item[{{\bf t\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-Datatype}}]{datatype, }
\item[{int}]{source, }
\item[{int}]{tag, }
\item[{{\bf t\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-Comm}}]{comm, }
\item[{{\bf t\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-Request} $\ast$}]{request}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{include_2thread__mpi_2tmpi_8h_a839030e4e95e6d349f4888697b5aee2c}
\-Initiate receiving a message.

\-This makes the buffer available to be filled with data. \-The contents of buf should not be relied on before the transmission is finished with \hyperlink{include_2thread__mpi_2tmpi_8h_a9cea5d5aad1d6b9d675d13cf9ff1acb7}{t\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-Wait()}, \hyperlink{include_2thread__mpi_2tmpi_8h_aaed5bf4b83939eaec49c4a6ed594eb7e}{t\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-Test()} or \hyperlink{include_2thread__mpi_2tmpi_8h_a2d09de79a46a51f0ddecff38410e261f}{t\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-Waitall()}.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{\-Parameters}

\hline

\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em tag} & \-The message tag (or \-T\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-A\-N\-Y\-\_\-\-T\-A\-G). \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em comm} & \-The shared communicator. \\
\hline

\-Initiate sending a message, non-\/blocking.

\-This makes the buffer available to be received. \-The contents of buf should not be touched before the transmission is finished with \hyperlink{include_2thread__mpi_2tmpi_8h_a9cea5d5aad1d6b9d675d13cf9ff1acb7}{t\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-Wait()}, \hyperlink{include_2thread__mpi_2tmpi_8h_aaed5bf4b83939eaec49c4a6ed594eb7e}{t\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-Test()} or \hyperlink{include_2thread__mpi_2tmpi_8h_a2d09de79a46a51f0ddecff38410e261f}{t\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-Waitall()}.

\-Do an operation between all locally held buffers on all items in the buffers, and send the results to root.

\-Collective function.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{\-Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em sendbuf} & \-The operand parameters. \-Root may specify \-T\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-I\-N\-\_\-\-P\-L\-A\-C\-E, in which case recvbuf will hold the operand parameters. \\
\hline

\hline

\-Do an t\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-Reduce, but with the following assumption\-: recvbuf points to a valid buffer in all calling threads, or sendbuf has the value \-T\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-I\-N\-\_\-\-P\-L\-A\-C\-E (in which case the values of sendbuf may be changed in that thread).

\-This avoids unnecesary memory allocations associated with the normal t\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-Reduce.

\-Collective function.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{\-Parameters}

\hline

\hline

\hline

\-Send \& receive message at the same time.

\-Blocks until recvbuf is filled, and sendbuf is ready for reuse.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{\-Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em sendbuf} & \-The buffer with data to send. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em sendcount} & \-The number of items to send. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em sendtype} & \-The data type of the items in send buf. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em dest} & \-The rank of the destination thread. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em sendtag} & \-The send message tag. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt out}  & {\em recvbuf} & \-The buffer for data to receive. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em recvcount} & \-The maximum number of items to receive. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em recvtype} & \-The data type of the items in recvbuf. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em source} & \-The rank of the source thread (or \-T\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-A\-N\-Y\-\_\-\-S\-O\-U\-R\-C\-E). \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em recvtag} & \-The recveive message tag (or \-T\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-A\-N\-Y\-\_\-\-T\-A\-G). \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em comm} & \-The shared communicator. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt out}  & {\em status} & \-The received message status. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{\-Returns}
\-T\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-S\-U\-C\-C\-E\-S\-S on success, \-T\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-F\-A\-I\-L\-U\-R\-E on failure. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{\-Returns}
\-T\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-S\-U\-C\-C\-E\-S\-S on success, \-T\-M\-P\-I\-\_\-\-F\-A\-I\-L\-U\-R\-E on failure. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
